When I checked in, Simon, a boy with glasses at the front desk, recommended the hotel cruise to us. The price was reasonable and it was very good. The cruise was carefully decorated and the night view of Jiaxing was very beautiful. We drove along the Grand Canal to the Nanhu Scenic Area and saw the red boat of the First National Congress of the Communist Party of China, which was a surprise. Simon also recommended that we go on the cruise to try the hotel's buffet restaurant seafood dinner, all-you-can-eat hairy crabs, and strongly recommend their drunken crabs, love it! In short, this hotel is very cost-effective and suitable for short-distance family trips. Highly recommended!!!
